Yan Huiqing's Speech in London on China's Plan for Japan

Applying Pressure to Japan to Accept the League of Nations Report

Consolidating China's Economic and Political Status and Implementing Long-Term Resistance

Expressing Gratification at the Change in British Attitude

(London) At a League of Nations Union banquet today, Yen Hui-ching delivered a speech, stating that the League of Nations Assembly's report on the Manchurian problem will be recorded in history as one of the most important documents in striving for international peace, justice, and fairness. Japan's aggression has overturned the balance of power in the Far East. If this balance is not restored, there will be extremely serious developments in the Pacific. Japan's past and present military activities in the Northeast are greatly disturbing world peace. China has not been able to exercise its rights under Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant, and for other reasons, has not been able to express its legitimate anger. However, this absolutely does not mean that China is willing to accept the established situation or recognize a situation created by force and considered by the civilized world to be completely incompatible with the general provisions of international law. The plan that China must adopt is: 1) China must exert pressure on Japan to accept the League of Nations Assembly's report; 2) China must find ways to consolidate its economic and political position so that it can prolong its resistance against Japan. He is very pleased to see that the attitude of the United Kingdom towards this matter has recently changed. This is because the United Kingdom is gradually realizing that, in addition to upholding the League of Nations resolution, for its own interests, especially in the current era of economic panic, it is imperative to pay attention to the possibility of China as the only major market and investment site. British trade with China currently accounts for only 2% of the United Kingdom's total foreign trade, and there is a real need for expansion. The development of Sino-British commercial relations will not only benefit the United Kingdom, but also enable the United Kingdom to implement a part of the League of Nations report's provisions. Dr. Yen finally mentioned the generous treatment received by the Chinese delegation to the World Economic Conference in the United Kingdom, saying that this has created an unforgettable impression. (Reuters, 14th)

County Magistrate Concurrently Serving as Military Judge in Bandit Suppression Areas

(Nanchang) The Headquarters has formulated the following Provisional Regulations for County Magistrates Concurrently Serving as Military Judges in Bandit Suppression Areas:

Article 1: For the purpose of rectifying military discipline and eliminating bandit troubles in all counties within the bandit suppression area, the magistrates of each county may be concurrently appointed as military judges by this Headquarters.

Article 2: If officers and soldiers stationed in each county violate military discipline or disrupt local order when going out, the concurrently serving military judge may correct them. If the circumstances are serious, they may be arrested. The direct superior officer shall be notified on one hand, and this Headquarters shall be reported on the other hand.

Article 3: If officers or soldiers dispatched to each county on official duty commit the acts mentioned in Article 2, in addition to being handled in accordance with regulations, the facts shall be directly reported to this Headquarters for review and handling.

Article 4: The concurrently serving military judge shall be responsible for investigating and handling any military personnel of unknown origin who linger within the borders of each county.

Article 5: The concurrently serving military judge may arrest and try the following categories of offenders: 1. Red bandits and brigands; 2. Non-military personnel who violate military laws and regulations; 3. Local traitors who disrupt public order.

Article 6: The concurrently serving military judge shall be guided by the Military Law Office of this Headquarters in the trial of cases. The judgment and execution of cases must be submitted to this Headquarters for approval before implementation.

Article 7: Scattered bandit captives captured by various units may also be sent to the concurrently serving county magistrate for trial.

Article 8: The county magistrate serving concurrently as military judge may establish auditors and clerks in the county government to assist in trial affairs. (Central News Agency, 14th)

(Nanchang) The Headquarters has ordered the reorganization of party affairs in various counties. Since these positions are unpaid, the use of official government structures is strictly prohibited to correct the bad habits of party offices and party officials. (Special Dispatch, 14th)

Complete Withdrawal Within Ten Days

The Japanese troops in Miyun and other areas must be completely withdrawn in the end.

The reorganized puppet troops in the received war zone will be processed separately.

Several negotiations with Japan since the Armistice Agreement

(Beiping Special Dispatch) The Japanese side recently claimed to our side that the Japanese troops within the war zone can be completely withdrawn within ten days, but the garrison in Miyun must be withdrawn in the end for two reasons: 1) There are still anti-Japanese organizations in Chahar; 2) The Japanese troops suffered extremely heavy casualties in the battle near Gubeikou, and the soldiers are grieving. The troops cannot be withdrawn until the remains of the fallen soldiers are properly buried. These statements from the Japanese side are all pretexts to delay the withdrawal of Japanese troops in Miyun and other areas. Therefore, there is extreme suspicion about whether the Japanese troops can be completely withdrawn within ten days, and special attention is paid to whether the Japanese troops in Miyun can be withdrawn for a while. In recent days, the Japanese troops near Ninghe on the east road and Tangshan and other places have begun to withdraw and concentrate in Luanzhou and Qinhuangdao. The Japanese troops in the Luanhe area are gradually withdrawing to Shanhaiguan and Jinzhou. There is still a regiment stationed near Lengkou, and there are also hundreds of people in Jianchangying. It is reported that the Japanese troops regard Jianchangying as an important fortress near Lengkou, and the Japanese troops there are not preparing to withdraw for the time being. The same is true for Xifengkou and Gubeikou. It is planned to station a portion of Japanese

troops in Santunying near Xifengkou and Shixia in Gubeikou to consolidate the defenses of the Great Wall line. The Japanese troops in Tongzhou, Sanhe, Xianghe, Yutian, Pinggu, Shunyi,

Page 12

etc., have already withdrawn completely. Except for Tongzhou and Shunyi, where order has been completely restored, the other counties have not been taken over. Local security is temporarily maintained by local people organizing their own militias. A few dozen Japanese troops are stationed in Jixian and Zunhua, etc., and they will be withdrawn soon. Most of the 8th Division of the Japanese Army in Gubeikou has retreated to Chengde. A regiment is stationed in Gubeikou, and two or three hundred people are in Miyun. A few dozen people have also been left in Huairou and have not been withdrawn. The withdrawal of the Japanese troops is extremely slow, and our side has not been able to take over smoothly due to the problems of the puppet troops. Since the meeting in Dalian, Xue Zhiheng and others have come to Beiping to discuss solutions. The handover procedures for the reorganization of the puppet troops and the Beining transportation war zone have all been in sight. The Reception Committee convened a meeting in Tianjin yesterday to discuss all the procedures and has distributed the work. Work will begin immediately. Regarding the reorganization of the puppet troops, Xue Zhiheng and Lei Shourong will be responsible for contacting and working with personnel sent by the Hebei Provincial Government to count and reorganize the troops. Xue and Lei will go to Tangshan immediately to make another contact with Li Jichun and then begin counting and reorganizing. The reception of the war zone east of Tangshan is planned to be guided by Yin Tong and Li Zeyi, accompanied by the county magistrates and public security chiefs to take over. Tao Shangming will be responsible for negotiating with the Japanese side and guiding the receiving personnel to receive the counties in Pingdong and Pingbei in sequence. Qian Zongze and Liu Shisun will be responsible for the opening of the Beining railway. The railway will be opened to Luozhou first, and then will seek to reach Shanhaiguan directly. As for the sorting out of the war zone and the internal affairs of the Reception Committee, Yu Xuezhong and Wei Jian will be responsible for presiding over them. The reception of the war zone can begin immediately and is expected to be completed within a month.

The establishment of the Armistice Agreement and the end of the war this time was a painful act of tolerance that was taken only as a last resort. Since the signing of the Armistice Agreement, the Chinese people have been swallowing their anger and the Japanese have been arrogant. The authorities felt extreme diplomatic difficulties in dealing with the agreement, and unexpected disputes that occurred temporarily were even more difficult to deal with. A weak country has no diplomacy. In order to seek a compromise, it had to be a tolerant submission. In the case of the shooting on the Dongdan tram, the Japanese side insisted that it was a provocation. After repeated negotiations, it finally ended with a formal apology to the Japanese side. In the case of the Japanese side arbitrarily arresting the Korean Independence Party leader Li Yongxiang in the public office of the capital, our side raised a negotiation with Japan on the basis of sovereignty, but the Japanese side ignored it and our side could do nothing. However, when the plainclothes leader Hao Peng was arrested in Tianjin, the Japanese side made a serious negotiation, threatening to use force. The authorities were afraid of creating difficulties and telegraphed the Tianjin local authorities to release him. This unpardonable traitor was released by the Japanese on the 9th with the help of the Japanese, and was taken to the Zhang Garden in the Japanese concession to continue his traitorous work. (13th)

Receiving War Zones Still Faces Many Difficulties

Difficult to Raise Funds for Assembled Pseudo-Troops

Shi Yousan's Forces Also Difficult to Resolve

Tianjin Special Dispatch: War Zone Receiving Committee members Xue Zhiheng, Yin Tong, and Lei Shourong went to Dalian to negotiate with the Japanese and puppet authorities regarding the reception of war zones. On the afternoon of the 8th, Xue, Yin, and Lei returned to Ping to report on their mission. News reporters from Tianjin and Beijing wanted to know the truth of the meeting to dispel the doubts of the people. It was recently learned that Lei and Yin were staying at No. 21 Haihe Road, Special District No. 1, Tianjin, in the Beining Road official residence, while Xue stayed at the Chongxing Company on Shou Street in the Japanese Concession. They went to their residences, but were all turned away. It was not until yesterday (the 11th) that they met Xue Zhiheng at the provincial government. After a few hasty words, Xue jumped into a car and left like a startled goose. The reporters then went to Haihe Road to visit Lei and Yin, but were still turned away. However, the reporters were sure that Lei and Yin were inside, so they were determined to see them. By this time it was already 6:30 PM. At 7:20 PM, the Japanese representative, Nagatsu, arrived in Tianjin. Lei and Yin had to go to the East Railway Station to welcome him. Fearing that the reporters would wait and not leave, preventing them from going out, Lei agreed to meet with them, saying that they had negotiated for a week in Dalian, but had not formed a meeting format. Everyone was casually chatting in their residences, barefoot and disheveled. There was nothing secret about the content. Because the Tanggu Truce was opposed by many, some out of patriotic indignation, and others for political reasons, the committee members agreed not to publish anything about the Dalian negotiations to avoid hindering the actual progress. They asked for everyone's understanding on this matter. At this point, Yin Tong interrupted, his face and physique closely resembling those of a foreigner, looking at his watch and saying, "There are still thirty minutes, we must go to the station." Yin's intention was to cut off Lei's talk before he got to the main point, so as to break the encirclement and leave. Unexpectedly, an ignorant servant chimed in, saying, "It only takes ten minutes to get to the East Station by car from here. If you leave now, you will still have to wait for twenty minutes." Yin and Lei looked at each other in silence, and then resumed the conversation with the reporters. However, they only revealed one or two things about the Dalian negotiations.

The Dalian negotiation records only exist in Japanese and not in Chinese (because no one has found the Chinese version). The content is divided into two main parts: (1) the disposition of the pseudo-troops and (2) the opening of the Tangshan-Yuguan section of the Beining Railway. Regarding the first item, Li Jichun's troops definitely have more than ten thousand men, but only three or four thousand firearms. The situation is that there are many officers but few soldiers, and many soldiers but few guns. Our side's reorganization standard is one person, one gun. Li did not insist on opposing the reorganization of four thousand men. The surplus personnel, both soldiers and officers, would be given twenty yuan and fifty yuan respectively and dismissed on the spot. The reorganized personnel would be formed into two police battalions, led by people recommended by Li, with salaries paid by our side for one month. Our side initially did not agree to this. All surplus officers and soldiers would be given twenty yuan each and dispersed in the Machang area. The two battalion commanders would need to be appointed by our side. The surplus firearms would be bought by us, with twenty yuan per large gun and fifty yuan per small gun. The title for Li was quite carefully considered. It is said that two methods are being considered: (1) giving him a corresponding position in the Beiping Military Affairs Commission, or (2) giving him the title of General Supervisor of War Zone Police Training. However, it is not yet fully determined. This is why Xue Zhiheng needs to go to Tangshan again to meet with Li for a final consultation. However, this is a minor issue and should not be difficult to resolve. The next issue is the funding for the reorganization, which will require at least three to four hundred thousand yuan. The central government hopes that Hebei Province will raise the funds itself, but Hebei Province is too impoverished to do so. Therefore, the committee members hope to start the reorganization on the 15th and complete it before the 25th, and then take over the political power of the counties, completing the entire reception within this month. Little do they know that reorganization is easy, but raising funds is difficult. In general, the reorganization will start on the 15th, but it may be difficult to achieve in reality. Regarding the second item, the opening of the Tangshan-Yuguan section of the Beining Railway, the inside story was quite complicated during the Dalian negotiations, not as simple and optimistic as rumored. Our side plans to open the railway to Luanzhou in the first step after Li's troops are resolved, and to Beidaihe in the second step. Opening the railway from Beidaihe to Yuguan still faces difficulties. Our side hopes that Li's troops will leave the railway line after reorganization and be stationed in Fengrun and Luanxian to avoid interfering with railway administration. However, although this is what we hope, it remains questionable whether it can be achieved in reality. In addition, there is an even greater difficulty, namely that during the Tianjin Incident of the previous year, Shi Yousan purchased 50,000 firearms from Japan. Japan sold them at half price because they benefited from Shi's disturbance in Tianjin. Three months ago, Shi went to Qinhuangdao and established a military cadre school there, training junior officers and hiring Japanese military instructors. There are a total of 1,500 students, mostly young graduates of middle and small schools recruited from outside the customs. Shi was not mentioned at all in the Dalian talks, which is regrettable. According to Lei and Yin, they hope that Shi's troops can be incorporated into Li's troops for resolution. However, it remains questionable whether this can be achieved in reality. If we look at Luandong, which is shaped like an enclave (and Luansi is no different), the Japanese do not care, Shi does not comply, and our side cannot reach him, what can be done? According to another source, it would not be difficult for our side to open the railway to Yuguan, as long as we agree to joint operations with the puppet Fengshan Railway. If we agree to this, wouldn't it be absurd? But how things will ultimately turn out remains to be seen as events unfold. (July 12)

Traitor Hao Peng Regains Freedom

Japanese Consul in Tianjin Protests, Diplomatic Atmosphere Extremely Bad

Diwei Road Suddenly Under Temporary Martial Law

Cars Carrying Hao Enter Japanese Concession

Tianjin Special Dispatch: The traitor Hao Peng was seized by his subordinates Yuan and Li at dawn on the 6th of this month and taken to the First Army Corps headquarters. The people were overjoyed, expecting that even if he was not beheaded, he would certainly be shot, and at the very least, he would be strangled like the Shanghai traitor Hu Lifu, leaving a complete corpse. Who knew that things would go completely wrong, contrary to expectations? Hao has actually regained his freedom. The details of what happened are as follows:

Hao Peng, having been sold into prison by his subordinates, knew that his crimes were heinous and could not be tolerated by the law. Therefore, he asked people everywhere to intercede for him, hoping to save his life and be sentenced to life imprisonment. On the one hand, he made extremely cunning confessions to the military court, vaguely saying that his organization was absolutely not for treason, but against non-resistance, dissatisfied with the current political situation, and intended to use foreign forces to improve politics and protect the country. Because he lived in the Japanese Concession, he was ignorant and isolated, no different from being trapped in a gourd, being played with without knowing it. Furthermore, many people said that the troops in North China had matured to 200,000 men, and as long as a signal flare was fired, there would be responses from all sides. A lot of money was spent on the movement. He thought that the Japanese were not fools, and they would not be willing to spend so much money without being certain of success. He also said that he recruited 2,000 plainclothes agents in the Japanese Concession and issued firearms on May 19, mostly hand grenades. The first person to throw a hand grenade would be given 100 yuan, and then 50 yuan per day. That night, only two or three hundred plainclothes agents were sent out, and only a few dozen returned. Most of the others threw their hand grenades aside and fled in the night. Not a single soldier responded. Only then did he realize that these people were unreliable, but he was in a situation where he could not back down, like an arrow on the string. So he continued to do it for a few more nights, but still failed. As for Chairman Yu's diligence and integrity, he admired him very much and always loved and respected him. He knew nothing about anyone plotting to assassinate Chairman Yu, and so on.

After Hao Peng was detained, many frustrated politicians lobbied and pleaded for him. He was taken to the military court at 10 AM on July 6. The Japanese consul in Tianjin, Tanaka, went to the provincial government to see Chairman Yu and protested against the arrest of people across the border, which was presumptuous. Yu said that his subordinates had mutinied and sent him in for a reward. He was a wanted criminal by the central government, and he would naturally take him in. He had telegraphed the central government for instructions. Tanaka said that there was no need to argue about this for the time being, and he would wait for the investigation before saying anything else. Before the investigation was clear, he must not dispose of Hao to avoid him dying without proof. Yu told him that he would not dispose of him without authorization. Tanaka also requested to meet with Hao for a talk, which Yu politely declined. At 3 PM the next afternoon, the commander of the Japanese Concession military police (also a staff officer of the garrison headquarters), Major Mori, fully armed, arrived at the provincial government by car. First he asked to see Chairman Yu, and then he wanted to meet with Hao Peng. Since Yu was out on official business, no one was in charge, and Mori left angrily. From the third day onwards, even more people interceded for Hao. At that time, the Japanese side had already settled the matter in the former capital. Yu was forced by circumstances and could do nothing. Therefore, three solutions were decided: (1) send him to Beiping for disposal, (2) hand him over to the court for trial, and (3) have him sentenced to life imprisonment by the military court. However, none of these three solutions were approved by Beiping, and the diplomatic atmosphere was very bad, saying that if Hao was not released, the reception of the war zones would be hindered. Therefore, weighing the importance of the matter, he had to release the prisoner and cancel the arrest warrant to complete the official procedures. On the evening of the 10th, the Japanese Concession side repeatedly called, urging his release. On the morning of the 11th, Hebei Diwei Road, Dajing Road, Dahutong, and Dongma Road were temporarily under martial law. At that moment, several cars drove into the Japanese Concession, followed by a burst of applause and cheers, and Hao Peng regained his freedom. (Written by Caofu on the 12th)

Southern Route Bandit Suppression Troops

The Seventh and Eighth Divisions Advance to Liuche and Sanbiao

The Second Division's Military Reputation Causes Bandits Attacking Chongshiwei to Collapse

Guangzhou Dispatch: The military affairs of the southern route bandit suppression troops have recently made considerable progress. The Guangdong army has repeatedly come into contact with bandits in the past month. The bandit gangs in the areas near Junmenting and Anyuan are still attacking the official army's defense lines from time to time. The bandits gathered in the Junmenting area are particularly numerous. The Xie Regiment of the Eighth Division of the Guangdong Army advanced toward Sanbiao on the 4th of this month. About three or four hundred bandits in the area resisted slightly and fled north. The Xie Regiment then occupied Sanbiao. At the same time, the 19th Regiment of the Seventh Division advanced toward Liuche, which belongs to Huichang, on the 6th. The red bandits in Liuche fled upon hearing the news. For the sake of caution, the 19th Regiment temporarily stationed on the high ground outside Liuche to prevent a bandit counterattack. While the various units of the Second Detachment were stationed in the Liuche and Sanbiao area, the First Column also sent troops to advance along the Anyuan line in order to establish contact with the Seventh and Eighth Divisions of the Second Detachment. However, fierce battles with bandits in the northeastern areas of Anyuan have been quite intense in recent days. Fortunately, Chen Jing's 32nd Regiment of the Fourth Division of the Second Army transferred the troops stationed in Longbu back to join the suppression, and the bandits attacking Chongshiwei were defeated. According to a telegram from Commander Chen from the front line yesterday, the bandits attacking Chongshi had retreated at night on the (3rd). According to prisoners Zhan Hongjiao and others, they were originally old troops of Chen Cheng, captured and serving in the Second Independent Division of the puppet Third Army Corps. The division had the 7th, 8th, and 9th Regiments. The 7th and 8th Regiments arrived after five days of marching from Ruijin and attacked Chongshi Xinwei. After charging eight times and suffering more than a hundred casualties, they retreated at night with the 22nd Division of the puppet Third Army and the Ruijin Model Regiment. The 22nd Division had three regiments, each with four companies, and each company had seventy or eighty rifles with forty or fifty rounds of ammunition per rifle. They arrived after four days of marching from Junmenting. On the morning of the 2nd, they encountered the national army and were bombed and attacked by the national army's hand grenades and light machine guns, suffering three or four hundred casualties. They saw that the national army's strength was too great and that the old fort could not be approached, so they retreated, etc. It was also reported that the bandits retreated in two directions on winter nights, one through Yanghu and one through Jingbei to Jinsha. The whole team had about three thousand remaining bandits, who retreated from Jinsha to Menhe. More than two hundred bandits were wounded and boarded boats at Shuidong. In this battle, the First Column suffered several platoon leader casualties and more than thirty soldier casualties. The Fourth Division of the Second Army has now sent troops to the Guanpu area, which is less than five miles from Anyuan. (9th)

Songjiang Drives Away Evil Spirits, Burning Ten Fingers

Luo Rongxing, a resident of Lujia Bridge in the southern gate of this city,

is a tailor. His wife, Luo Jiang, suffers from neurasthenia.

Sometimes she is possessed by evil spirits, and she raves day and night. After waking up, she is physically exhausted, almost like a serious illness. The year before last, her husband learned a method of exorcism and tried it, tightly striking her fingertips with a thread and burning them with moxa, which proved to be surprisingly effective and did not recur for two years. Unexpectedly, recently she suddenly relapsed. Rongxing followed the old method, tying his wife to a pillar and burning her with moxa, locking her in a room. Although she screamed in pain, he did not care. When a neighbor, He Laosan, passed by and heard the terrible screams, he went inside to investigate and saw that all ten fingers had been burned. He immediately released her. Everyone felt resentment at Luo Rongxing's inhumane behavior and reported it to a branch police station for investigation. Yesterday, he was transferred to the county court prosecutor's office for examination of the injuries. The official ordered Luo Rongxing to be detained, but Luo Jiang could not bear to see her husband in prison and only asked that he be ordered to send her to a doctor for treatment. According to reports, Luo Rongxing agreed to treat her in court, and the detention order was revoked. Luo Rongxing has already sent the injured Luo Jiang to the hospital for treatment.

Suzhou Wujiang Murder Case Requests Steaming Bones for Examination

Tang Shoufu, a villager in Shao Angcai Township, Wujiang County, suddenly died of a violent illness. After investigation by his father, Tang Yongxiang,

it was learned that Tang Shoufu's wife, Hang, colluded with her lover to murder him. According to Tang Fuxin, Shoufu's four-year-old daughter, she was strangled by Hang, etc. Therefore, Tang Yongxiang petitioned the High Court Prosecutor's Office and ordered the Wuxian District Court to send a coroner to open the coffin for examination. Because the body was already decomposed, it was difficult to examine it for a time. Hang and others were detained. Tang Yongxiang hired lawyer Shen Yuan yesterday (the 14th) to draft a petition to the High Prosecutor's Office to conduct a bone-steaming examination in order to redress the injustice.

Actively Widening Gong Lane and Ganjia Lane

The county government has approved the construction and widening of Gong Lane, Ganjia Lane, and Songhebanchang Street in the city. Preparations have been completed, and construction will begin on August 1. At the same time, the owners of the houses on both sides are required to demolish them all before the end of July to facilitate the project. After this road is widened, cars from the train station to the public enclosure can go directly, and cars can pass through both inside and outside the city.

Wuxi Yixing Man Drowns Himself in the River

Xiaojishan, Kaiyuan Township, Fourth District, is located on the shore of Taihu Lake, with beautiful scenery. Recently, with the arrival of summer and the blooming of lotus flowers,

there are many tourists. Around 9 PM the night before last, two cars carrying several richly dressed tourists came to Xiaojishan for relaxation. At that time, a man of about twenty years old was wandering alone near the Lirang Bridge in Xiaojishan. Before long, the richly dressed tourists all returned home after having their fill of enjoyment. Around 11 PM, villagers Yao Langen and two others suddenly saw a paper package beside the Lirang Bridge, containing a long gown, gauze skirt, toothbrush, letter, steel yuan, pencil, and white leather shoes, etc. Yao immediately reported the information to Gu Jinyuan and asked police officer Kong Fanmao to report it to the Third Police Station of the Ninth Branch Bureau, which sent police chief Huang Ronggui to investigate. There were no other traces. Until 8 AM yesterday, a corpse was seen floating on the surface of the river at Lirang Bridge. Zhuyi Ji, the chief of the district, reported it to the county court. Chief Zhou led officials to conduct an autopsy and confirmed that it was a case of drowning. After the autopsy, the district chief prepared a coffin for burial. It is said that the deceased was from Heqiao, Yixing, named Xu Dongsheng (also known as Yu Ren). His belongings are temporarily stored in the court.

Agricultural Bank Teller Detained for Embezzlement

Xi Chuanshu (also known as Juchu), a teller at the Shanghai Agricultural and Industrial Bank, embezzled more than 3,000 yuan from the bank in May of this year and secretly came to Wuxi, hiding at No. 4 Niansi, Taiping Bridge in the city. This was discovered by the bank, which then petitioned the First Special District Court to order bailiffs Cheng Renkun and Liu Qinglan to come to Wuxi with documents and report to the county court for police assistance in the arrest. They went together to arrest Xi at 6 PM the day before yesterday and arrested him on the spot. Yesterday, he was escorted to Shanghai to be brought to justice.

Two More Murder Cases Occur in the Urban Area

Zhang Hengshan, a salt merchant from Yancheng who lived at No. 2, Daheshang, in the city, was 44 years old and made a living pulling a rickshaw. His wife, Chen, was 42 years old and had one son and five daughters. Yesterday (the 14th) morning at 9 AM, Hengshan bought rice and vegetables and went home. While passing by the gate of Qin Boxian, a resident there, the large tree in front of Qin's gate suddenly broke and fell. Hengshan was unable to avoid it and was crushed, his brains splattered and his left leg broken. He died shortly after. His wife, Chen, upon hearing the news, mourned over his body and fainted several times. It was a tragic sight. Also, Yang Meidi, a female worker in the fine yarn room of the Shenxin Yarn Factory outside the west gate, was 17 years old. Yesterday (the 14th) morning at 10 AM, she was pushed in the chest by Xia Xiaohai, a male worker in the same factory, and fell to the ground, dying instantly. The factory has posted a notice offering a coffin allowance of 40 yuan to show sympathy, but the workers have expressed dissatisfaction and went to the county party headquarters to petition at 12 PM, demanding that the factory offer more generous compensation.

Chen Jinbao, instructor of the Jintongqiao Beihudai

Security Corps in the First District, privately stole firearms

last autumn and, together with bandits Fan Genbao and Wu Hanwen, burned and looted the homes of Chen Zhang and Wang Xiao, killing police officer Wu Qi at the back gate of the Public Security Bureau. He was arrested in Wuxi last month, and after a clear confession, he was reported to the provincial government and approved for execution. It was carried out at noon on the 13th.

number of anti-Japanese yarns by the Anti-Japanese

Association. Later, Xie Zian (a middle school teacher in the county) bribed Yue Xishan of the association with 400 yuan. Yue reported him, and Xie was handed over to the court for trial. Yang Shaozhen, deputy manager of the Lihua Factory, arrived and hired lawyer Chen Dayou to appear in court for defense. Xie Zian hired lawyer Xu Yuxiang for defense. The plaintiff Yue Xishan and witnesses Zhang Fusheng, a tea room attendant, etc., all appeared in court. The judge was Wang Decheng. After questioning the plaintiffs and defendants, the lawyers began to debate. As a result, the court ordered Yang Shaozhen to pay a cash deposit of 1,000 yuan and a written guarantee of 2,000 yuan for release. Xie Zian was remanded in custody, and the debate was declared over. After the court adjourned, the staff of the Anti-Japanese Association and the audience expressed dissatisfaction with lawyer Chen Dayou's defense of the treacherous merchants and waited at the entrance of the court, preparing to drag him through the streets to vent their anger. Nantong Lusi Hurricane Sweeps People Away and Tears Down Houses

Lusi, on the Huanghai coast of Nantong, has seen repeated

disasters recently. Around 9 AM yesterday, the sky was dark, and a

sudden hurricane arose, with leaves and reed shavings flying in the air. Gu Dequan, a sugar seller from Taizhou, was swept up into the air by the strong wind near the Laihe Bridge, and then fell down, but was not injured. Zhou Jinkou, a rickshaw puller from Lusi, was 30 years old. He was passing east of the Laihe Bridge when he was blown into the air and fell west of the bridge, injuring his leg. Suddenly, a large panel door flew over and hit his head and chest, causing serious injuries. Zhai Henian, the head of Zhongzheng Township, who runs the Dada Automobile Company, had his five houses swept away by the wind without a trace, and not even a single tile remained. Li San, who pushes a cart, also had his two thatched cottages disappear. At the same time, terrifying waves in the sea were like mountains falling, causing people to feel frightened. The Public Security Bureau submitted the disaster situation to the county government on the 13th for investigation and disaster relief.

On the morning of the 12th, locusts flew through Langshan Port in Nantong, heading east, with a few landing. The Public Security Bureau cooperated with farmers to exterminate them. despite having petitioned the Ministry of Finance to order salt merchants to allocate

funds from the salt permit surtax, they have not complied, causing financial difficulties for various institutions to reach their limit. was over forty years old and worked as a plasterer. His wife,

Director of Navigation Department Comes to Shanghai to Thoroughly Investigate the Tunan Incident

Investigating the Issue of Responsibility in Detail

And Seriously Negotiating with the Japanese Side

Following the collision and sinking of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tunan ship by the Japanese Dalian Steamship Company's Changchun Maru, the Ministry of Transportation yesterday specially dispatched the Director of the Navigation Department, Gao Tingzi, to Shanghai to thoroughly investigate the issue of responsibility for the incident in order to make serious representations to the Japanese side. According to Gao, the loss of the Tunan ship is limited to the ship itself, while the lives of the crew and passengers, as well as the future safety of Chinese ships, are extremely serious issues. Therefore, the Ministry of Transportation specially sent him to Shanghai to conduct a thorough investigation. If the Japanese ship is responsible, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will make serious representations in order to protect maritime lives. As for the names and numbers of the crew members, it has been determined that there are 56 crew members, with 29 missing. The number of passenger deaths and losses has yet to be estimated and will be confirmed when the Tianjin Maru arrives in Shanghai. Based on the current investigation, the Japanese Changchun Maru should be held responsible for this unfortunate incident. The location of the collision was in the Shandong waters not far from Qingdao. At that time, the Tunan ship was sailing on a straight line to Tianjin, while the Changchun Maru was sailing on a diagonal line. There is no doubt that the collision was caused by the Changchun Maru's incorrect route. However, the detailed situation will be clarified after the rescued crew members arrive in Shanghai and are questioned.

Sending Personnel to Care For

The 89 crew and passengers rescued from the Tunan ship,

are permitted

to come to Shanghai on the Dalian Steamship Company's Tianjin Maru.

The ship departed from Dalian at 1:00 PM yesterday, stopping first at Qingdao, then coming to Shanghai. Yesterday, it was telegraphed that the Tianjin Maru is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 7:00 AM tomorrow morning. The rescued personnel will disembark at the Huangpu Wharf. Yesterday, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company dispatched eight staff members to the wharf tomorrow morning to care for them. At the same time, Jun'an Society was instructed to temporarily accommodate the sailors and stokers. The passengers will be cared for by Qian Mingshu and others and be ready to meet upon arrival.

The 39 boxes of silver ingots and

silver dollars inside the ship,

worth more than 200,000

yuan, were loaded in Yantai by the

local Bank of Communications and unfortunately also sank. However, the silver treasures are all covered by marine insurance. The insurance companies are now in agreement to proceed with salvage procedures and are investigating the sea area where the Tunan sank, which is about 50 to 60 feet deep, so it is possible to salvage the silver boxes.

Mr. Zeng Yijing Returns to Shanghai Yesterday Morning After the Long-Distance Flight Along the Yangtze River

Discussing the many experiences gained on this trip

Saving the country through aviation requires training talent

The Jiangfeng aircraft's pontoon slightly damaged, already transported to Shanghai

According to Riri News, Zeng Yijing, director of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau, departed from Shanghai on the 15th of last month with German pilot Buri on the domestically produced Jiangfeng seaplane trainer for a long-distance flight along the Yangtze River. After reaching Yuezhou, the pontoon was slightly damaged, and it was returned to Hankou for repairs. It was transported back to Shanghai on the Jianguo ship, and Mr. Zeng also took the ship east, arriving at the port at 11:00 AM yesterday morning. A reporter from Riri News specifically went to see Mr. Zeng at the bureau yesterday and learned the following:

Flight Experience

According to Mr. Zeng, he promoted

domestically produced aircraft to awaken

his compatriots. In mid-last month, he piloted

the Jiangfeng aircraft on a

long-distance flight along the Yangtze River. This flight was not difficult. When arriving in Zhenjiang, the aircraft's pontoon was slightly damaged, and he immediately telegraphed for workers to come from Shanghai for repairs. He then continued flying, passing through Nanjing, Wuhu, Anqing, Jiujiang, Wuxue, and other places. On the 20th, he arrived in Hankou. Because the current of the Yangtze River was very rapid, reaching a speed of five miles per hour, the connection of the aircraft's pontoon was damaged again. He immediately had it hoisted onto the Weisheng gunboat for repairs, which took three or four days. On the 29th, he flew to Yuezhou. He originally planned to fly to Changsha, reaching Shashi and Yichang. The river flow upstream from Hankou increased by two miles per hour. He reluctantly flew back to Hankou on the 6th of this month. The aircraft was still able to fly with difficulty, but the German pilot, for the sake of caution, did not fly east again. He disassembled the aircraft and transported it back to Shanghai on the Jianguo ship.

Training Talent

Mr. Zeng continued, "Although this flight was not fully successful, it should

break the Chinese people's belief in foreign-made aircraft.

Our bureau's domestically produced aircraft has a sturdy fuselage made of steel. Otherwise, it would have been scattered and destroyed by the impact of the river. This trip has provided a lot of experience, and in the future, we will strive to rebuild and seek to strengthen the interior and the pontoon. Then, even if we encounter strong winds and huge waves, we will not be affected. I believe that saving the country through aviation does not lie in simply buying aircraft, but in awakening the general youth who are willing to receive aviation education and provide them with good training. In ten years, our country's aviation will be very promising. Our country's current aviation talents are all flying low-speed aircraft and have no combat skills."

Continuing to Fly South

Mr. Zeng also said, "The Jiangfeng aircraft has now been

shipped back for repairs, which should be

completed within two months. After the repairs are completed, it will fly to the

outer port of Wusong as a field test. I am not discouraged and will continue to work hard to make a long-distance flight along the coast. Ningbo, Wenzhou, Fuzhou, and Xiamen all have inland ports where it can be moored. However, we must prepare for any unexpected events, so that if an accident occurs, it can land on the sea. If the aircraft's pontoon is not strong, it will be impacted by the waves and sink."

Hosting Journalists

Mr. Zeng believes that it is necessary to report the experiences of this flight

to all sectors.

He specifically scheduled a meeting at 10:00 AM this morning at the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau in Gaochang Temple to provide a detailed report to the local press.

Bringing promotional materials and establishing contact with foreign reporters stationed in Shanghai. In addition, he brought a large number of promotional materials, entrusted to Diao Minqian, a representative of our country to the Pacific Conference, to be distributed to representatives of various countries in order to promote the political situation and construction plans of our country. It is learned that Mr. Li has completed his official duties and is scheduled to return to Beijing on the overnight express train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway tonight.

Ministry of Finance Investigates Auxiliary Currency in Various Provinces

When the new currency was issued, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce petitioned the Ministry of Finance to reorganize auxiliary currency. The Ministry of Finance is planning this matter and is starting by investigating the types of auxiliary currency circulating in various provinces. The investigation of the types of auxiliary currency in each province revealed that there are 15 types of bronze, silver, and paper auxiliary currency in Jiangsu. The types of auxiliary currency used in Jiangsu include double silver coins from Guangdong, Jiangnan, Hubei, and Beiyang, while single silver coins are extremely rare. Zhejiang double coins include those from Guangdong and Fujian, while single silver coins are also rare. Anhui is the same as Jiangsu. Jiangxi double coins include those from Guangdong. Most are auxiliary currency notes. Hubei double coins include those from Guangdong, Jiangnan, and Hubei. Single coins include one type of Yuan Shikai. Hunan has very few Guangdong double coins in the south, with no other circulation. Guangdong single and double coins include one type from Guangdong. Guangxi double coins include those from Guangdong and Guangxi, with no single silver coins. Fujian double coins include those from Fujian and Guangdong. Single coins include two types of Yuan Shikai and Guangdong, as well as local one and two silver dollar coins. Guangzhou double coins include two types from Guangdong and Yuan Shikai, and a few half-dollar coins. Yunnan has very few silver auxiliary coins, with most circulation being copper auxiliary coins. Henan has a few Yuan Shikai single silver coins, while double coins are very rare. There are also 200-500 large copper coins each. Shanxi is the same as Henan. Hebei double coins include three types from Hubei, Jiangnan, and Yuan Shikai. Single silver coins include three types from Jiahe, Hubei, and Jiangnan. Shandong has very few double silver coins. Shaanxi has Yuan Shikai dragon and phoenix single and double silver coins, and Sichuan Shengyuan silver coins. Sichuan half-dollar silver coins are of two types from Sichuan and Yunnan. Single and double silver coins are very rare. Auxiliary currency is not circulated in Suiyuan, Chahar, Jilin, or Heilongjiang. Liaoning has a few dragon and phoenix single and double coins.

Silk Factory Workers in the Concession Resume Work Yesterday Morning

Negotiations on Wage Issues at the Shuanggong Factory Fail to Reach a Result

Due to the factory's agreement to pay back wages, all workers in the silk factory strike in the concession area of this city resumed work as usual yesterday morning. Workers at the Fulun Shuanggong Factory at the end of Hongri Tianbao Road continued to strike yesterday. The details are recorded separately below:

Resumption of Work in the Concession Approximately 2,000 workers from the five factories in the concession area, namely Yuanhe, Chunji, Jingwei, Taichang on Alabastor Road, Xiangyuan on Gansu Road, and Qianyu on Manzhou Road, believed that the June wages of 45 cents per day violated the social mediation decision, causing a backlash. They announced a strike one after another the day before yesterday. The Second District Silk Workers Union sent personnel to negotiate, and the factories agreed to uniformly pay the outstanding five cents for June on the 16th of this month. Yesterday morning at 4:30 AM, Yang Shumei, Chen Lianxi, Cui Abao, A San, and others from the Third District Silk Workers Union went to various factories to persuade them to resume work. At that time, many workers gathered at the factory gates and were unwilling to enter the factory to work, stating that they would only resume work if the outstanding five cents for June were paid in full that day. The Third District Silk Workers Union feared that the dispute would be prolonged, and after consulting with the factory owners, the factory owners agreed. Therefore, the workers of each factory gradually entered the factory to resume work.

Shuanggong Remains Suspended More than 500 workers at the Fulun Shuanggong Silk Factory at the end of Hongkou Tianbao Road recently requested that wages be set at 50 cents per day, in accordance with the single-factory wage system. However, the factory did not allow it because the production of silk at the Shuanggong factory was simple and the selling price was low. Because the workers had not obtained their demands, they suddenly went on strike the day before yesterday (the 12th). Yesterday morning, directors Chen Xiupu and Lu Xusheng went to the factory to discuss a solution with manager Shen Zubei. The factory stated that the output of the Shuanggong factory was of poor quality and the selling price was low. If wages were paid according to the single-factory wage system, it would be difficult to maintain. However, it agreed to increase wages by two cents per day, changing it to 47 cents. However, the workers insisted on 50 cents per day, resulting in no result. All workers continued to strike yesterday, and it is feared that a resolution will be difficult to achieve.

Already the Municipal Government Negotiating with the French Consulate

And Sending Letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Federation of Labor for Assistance

The case of the Mei-Ya Ninth Weaving and Dyeing Factory on Xujiahui Road in the French Concession being ordered to stop night work by the French Municipal Council was yesterday reported to the Municipal Government and the Bureau of Social Affairs by the Shanghai Electrical Machinery and Silk Industry Association. They urged a swift and serious negotiation with the French Consul-General, and also sent letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Chinese Industrial Federation, requesting them to find ways to provide assistance in order to avoid destroying national goods factories and safeguarding labor administration. The original letter to the Municipal Government reads as follows: “We are reporting on the illegal order by the French Municipal Council to stop night work at the Mei-Ya Ninth Weaving and Dyeing Factory, a member of our association, which is causing losses to the factory's business and hindering the livelihood of workers. We are reporting the situation and urging negotiations to stop it. Our association received a letter from the member Mei-Ya Weaving and Dyeing Factory on the 8th of this month (omitted, see previous report in this newspaper) and so on. Based on this, we have investigated and found that the factory has been in operation for a long time, located in a remote area in the western suburbs of Shanghai, with very few nearby residents. Moreover, when the factory was established, it was inspected and approved by the French Works Department. The factory's night work has been in place for a long time. Residents who moved here later should have considered this themselves. Having moved in, how can they force the factory that was here first to stop working? The French Municipal Council's abrupt order to Mei-Ya to stop night work, citing disturbance to the sleep of nearby residents, is completely unreasonable. The factory pays taxes and operates lawfully in the French Concession. The French Municipal Council does not provide reasonable protection but instead indulges in illegal destruction, which is outrageous. While the Municipal Government is in the process of negotiating the management rights of factories in the concession, the French Concession Municipal Council is taking the lead in overstepping its authority. It has already ordered the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory to relocate and now orders Mei-Ya Silk Factory to stop night work. Its intention to damage our national goods industry is clearly sinister. Mei-Ya Silk Factory has suffered considerable losses due to this oppression, and the relationship to the infringement of our labor administrative rights is also very significant. In view of the above, we have prepared a document and respectfully request Your Excellency's review and approval, and urge you to swiftly negotiate with the French Consul-General, ordering the French Municipal Council to stop this action so as to secure industry and assert national rights. We are awaiting your orders with utmost urgency.”

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Again Telegrams the Executive Yuan to Maintain the Credit of the Arsenal's Mortgage Loan

National Debt Not Based on Civil Law Provisions

Is Truly Contrary to the Spirit of the Rule of Law

Xin Sheng She reports that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has again presented a case to the Executive Yuan to fight for the arsenal mortgage loan case. The letter is recorded as follows:

Chen Yi's Reply

Xiaolai, my dear friend, I received your letter of June 17, and have understood everything in detail. Upon investigation, there was a previous established case and there was no objection. Moreover, the merchants advanced a large sum of money, and the circumstances at the time were compelling. Therefore, their creditor rights and interests should be maintained. However, what needs to be reviewed is whether the debts owed as a result of the previous warlord infighting should be used as collateral for central government property. In summary, this case involves two issues: the mortgage and the debt. It concerns the authority of two ministries and has been reported to the Executive Yuan for submission to the Executive Conference for a decision. This is my reply.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Petition

To the Nanjing Executive Yuan: This chamber has reported that the mortgage rights of the Shanghai Arsenal base cannot be unilaterally denied according to law. On the 13th of this month, we received a reply from Vice Minister Chen of the Ministry of Military Affairs to Chairman Wang Xiaolai of this chamber (original text see previous report). After carefully reading it, we were even more shocked and astonished. The Ministry initially stated that the factory property belonged to the Ministry and could not be disposed of by local officials. However, when this chamber reported that the mortgage had been approved by the then Ministries of Finance and Army, the Ministry changed its tune again, saying that whether the debts of warlord infighting should be used as collateral for central government property was being questioned. In every possible way, they wanted to use administrative procedures to cancel the legally established mortgage contract. The state is not handling debt contracts in accordance with the provisions of the Civil Law, but instead resorting to administrative measures, hoping to use this to undermine the equal relationship between the parties so that they can dispose of the property freely. This is contrary to the spirit of the rule of law. Therefore, this chamber finds it difficult to accept the Ministry's intention to decide the existence or abolition of the mortgage contract through an administrative meeting. The taxes paid by the people during the era of warlord rule were all central government revenue. If we were to follow this logic, then all donations and taxes paid before the 16th year of the Republic would inevitably be invalid in order to be consistent in theory. In terms of the mortgage right itself, were the public bonds and treasury bills issued by the Beijing government not used for military expenses? Everyone knows that this is not the case. What guarantee was used for the tariff on bonds and treasury bills, and was not the tariff also central government property? How is it different from the arsenal base? Yet, one is being continuously fulfilled, while the other is being overturned. The treatment of debts from the same era of warlords can be so different, leading observers to suspect that there is no standard for right and wrong, and that judgments are based solely on the intentions of the authorities. This will further damage the state's clear governance. These advances, which were supposed to be secured, have not only not been repaid with principal and interest after ten years, but even the issue of whether the contract exists or not is still in dispute. Now, the Ministry claims on the one hand that it will maintain the interests of creditors, while on the other hand, it doubts whether the factory property should be used as collateral. If that is the case, it is tantamount to turning secured debt into unsecured debt. Taking today's 96 Bonds as an example, although the government has not issued a document to cancel or deny them, the principal and interest have not been paid, and they have long been in a state of limbo. I fear that the Ministry's so-called maintenance of creditors' interests will not be enough to reassure the creditors, and will be criticized as simply being empty words. As the chamber that handled this matter, we have no way to defend ourselves. Therefore, maintaining the interests of creditors and maintaining the mortgage are essentially the same thing, and it is difficult to separate them into two. Now, we are again telegraphing Your Yuan to request that you review and approve that we do not seek so-called ways to maintain creditors' rights other than destroying the contract, so as to demonstrate the state's clear governance. This would be most fortunate. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully bows. Yuan.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Advocates Universal Cancellation of Telephone Charges between Chinese and Concession Areas

Letter to the Works Department's Chinese Directors Urging Vigorous Promotion

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that every time telephones are used between the Chinese and Concession areas, a fee of five cents must be paid. The procedure is complicated and the burden on citizens is heavy. Therefore, yesterday it sent separate letters to the Shanghai Telephone Bureau and the Concession Telephone Company, requesting that the telephone charges be universally cancelled as soon as possible. At the same time, it also sent letters to the Chinese Directors of the Works Department, Yu Qiaqing, Xu Xinliu, Yuan Ludeng, etc., urging them to vigorously promote this matter during the meeting. The two letters are recorded separately below:

Letter to the Telephone Bureau

Dear Sirs, Regarding calls between the Chinese area telephone and the Concession telephone in this city, a telephone charge of five cents must be paid for every three minutes. This type of call within the same area requires users to bear an additional obligation to pay fees each time, in addition to the rent they should pay. This increases the burden on users. This is unreasonable and is an unprecedented example in various countries. Telephone users have always believed that this method was an expedient measure when manual switchboards were used at the time. It was originally hoped that the automatic switchboard would be upgraded in the future and that this fee would be cancelled. Now that your bureau has upgraded to an automatic switchboard, there is only a proposal to increase the price, and the method of charging five cents per call is still being implemented, which increases the burden on users and causes resentment. It does not seem to be a way for the company to take care of its users. When our association discussed with your bureau about not increasing the phone price, we also promised to find a way to cancel this matter. Recently, we have read in the newspapers that your bureau also has expressed its intention to automatically cancel this matter in the near future, which is a great relief to the public. However, we have not yet seen its effective implementation. We hereby send this letter to request that you investigate and decisively abolish the method of collecting five cents per call, so as to respond to the public's expectations. We look forward to it.

Letter to the Chinese Directors

Dear Sirs, Regarding the fact that telephone calls between the Chinese and Concession areas have always been charged a telephone fee of five cents, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, in order to reduce the burden on citizens, has repeatedly negotiated to cancel the telephone fee. However, it has not been implemented because it has not been approved by the Shanghai Telephone Company. It should be noted that the telephone lines between the Chinese and Concession areas have already been formally connected, and there is no obstruction to calls between them. The telephone fee is not necessary. We hereby send this letter to request that you consider proposing to cancel the aforementioned telephone fee of five cents at the same time as the Chinese area at the Board of Directors meeting of the Works Department, so as to benefit users. We will be deeply grateful.

丨 Still Handled According to Previous Rules 丨

The Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office has wanted to collect twice the amount since Ding Xie took over this year. After hearing the news, the tobacco and alcohol industries in this city rose up in opposition. The industry associations sent personnel to negotiate repeatedly. As a result, the office agreed to follow the old rules. The industry was satisfied. However, a few days ago, Renxing on Xibaoxing Road in Zhabei and Dashenchang on Fangxie Road in Nanshi and other stores were ordered to bring their licenses to the office to pay taxes and exchange them for new licenses. A certain collection director from the north and south offices detained the licenses, asking for four yuan for a license worth two yuan, almost causing a dispute. Fortunately, Teng Zhixiang and Tong Lingyun, the director of the Shanghai North Branch of the Tobacco Industry Association, went to the tax office to negotiate. Director Ding explained that it was a misunderstanding and promised to instruct the staff to handle the matter according to the previous practice and not to harass them again. The dispute was immediately resolved.

Lawyers Association Petitions for Protection of Lawyer Wang Shuchiao

Regarding his Brother Wang Yaqiao's Affair

Has Already Published a Statement in the Newspaper Severing Ties

The Shanghai Lawyers Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government, stating, "Dear Sirs, According to reports in the newspaper on the 9th of this month, lawyer Wang Shuchiao was suspected by the captured criminal Zhou Zhizhang of involvement in the assassination case of Tie Qiao, and was being held at the Shanghai First Special District District Court. The Municipal Public Security Bureau under your government has also sent a detective officer, team leader Gao Wansheng, to the court to request a transfer. Because the case has not progressed, the official document has not been submitted." "Lawyer Wang Shuchiao is a member of our association and has always been law-abiding and does not participate in external affairs since he started working as a lawyer. When the Zhao case occurred in July and August of the 19th year of the Republic, lawyer Wang Shuchiao was still living and studying at school during the Hassei era. Especially, he has no relation with any parties of society. After the news that he was framed was published in the newspapers, our association received repeated letters from Legislative Yuan member Zhao Chen and Executive Committee Alternate Tang Hao, Supervisory Committee Alternate, Tong Shi Ying, etc. who were raised at the meeting and then submitted to the 143rd Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees. After careful deliberation, it was unanimously agreed that the Zhao case had been investigated by the Public Concession Bureau and had been sent to the First Special District District Court for questioning twice. There were legal procedures to follow. Lawyer Wang was implicated for no reason and the truth would soon come to light. We should quietly wait for the judicial authorities to resolve the matter according to law, and our association should not express any opinion. It is suspicious why the Municipal Public Security Bureau is applying to the court to transfer him. It is worth mentioning that our association received a report from lawyer Wang on January 27 of this year, stating that on the 22nd of this month, a large number of detectives from the French Police Station suddenly entered and searched his residence at No. 351, Ladou Road in the French Concession, preventing people from entering and leaving until 6 p.m. the night before. It is rumored that this was initiated by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the bureau's note to the police station was in the name of checking the family of his brother Yaqiao. In fact, the member and his brother have long been living separately. His brother is viewed with suspicion by the authorities due to political relations. As a member, he has never engaged in any illegal activities. Whether in terms of law or reason, the Chinese and Concession authorities should not arbitrarily involve him or accuse him of crimes." "On the 31st, he received another report stating that according to rumors from outside, plainclothes detectives sent by the Shanghai Municipal Government Security Office, Public Security Bureau, and other agencies planned to take special measures to take the members to the Chinese area without notifying the police station, so as to force him to reveal the whereabouts of his brother. Although these rumors are not credible, there are still people resembling detectives patrolling near his residence, and servants are interrogated every time they enter and leave. It is evident that they have special purposes, and the members' bodies and families are in danger of being harmed. Thinking of this, he could not help but shudder. Considering that the member has been exclusively engaged in lawyer business since graduating from school, he has never participated in any political movements, and he has been living separately from his brother Yaqiao for a long time. Their actions are not known to each other. In terms of law and fact, Shuchiao is absolutely not jointly liable for his brother's actions. All of these matters can be reviewed. Even if Wang Yaqiao is suspected of committing a crime, it is clearly irrelevant to his brother, lawyer Wang Shuchiao. Moreover, according to the principle of no implication of family members, even though lawyer Wang is Wang Yaqiao's brother, he bears absolutely no responsibility for any crimes. How can he be arbitrarily implicated and arrested? The Municipal Public Security Bureau's application for transfer this time is inappropriate and should be protected by our association upon sending a letter to your government to inform its subordinate agencies." "Subsequently, on March 30, we received a reply stating that the Municipal Public Security Bureau reported that it had not sent anyone to spy on or search lawyer Wang Shuchiao's office, etc., which are all on file. Although the Municipal Public Security Bureau has issued a statement regarding the search of lawyer Wang's residence, the Chinese and Concession authorities believe that Wang Yaqiao's crimes are serious and have been unable to apprehend him. They are trying to detain his brother by any means to find out his brother's whereabouts in order to arrest him. The facts are clear and cannot be denied. However, our association believes that although lawyer Wang Shuchiao and Wang Yaqiao are brothers, one is nearly 50 years old while the other is only 26. There is a significant age difference. One is accustomed to revolutionary life, while the other is usually very careful and speaks gently. They are indeed conservative and law-abiding. Their personalities are also very different. They have been living separately for a long time and their actions have never been planned together. Several years ago, lawyer Wang once published a statement in the newspaper severing his brotherly relationship with Wang Yaqiao. All of these matters can be reviewed. Even if Wang Yaqiao is suspected of committing a crime, it is clearly irrelevant to his brother, lawyer Wang Shuchiao. Moreover, according to the principle of no implication of family members, even though lawyer Wang is Wang Yaqiao's brother, he bears absolutely no responsibility for any crimes. How can he be arbitrarily implicated and arrested? The Municipal Public Security Bureau's application for transfer this time is inappropriate and should be protected by our association upon sending a letter to your government to inform its subordinate agencies. The discussion was recorded on file. We hereby present the case and respectfully request your review and approval, adhering to the principle of fairness, and handling it according to the previous order No. 4538 of your government, protecting him and not transferring him. This would be convenient for the law." Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Government.

General Overview of Silk and Tea Production and Sales in Zhejiang and Anhui

This year's summer cocoons from various parts of Zhejiang Province, transported by the Hangzhou Railway, were shipped by the Huitong Company starting on the 29th of last month. Up to yesterday, there were about four thousand bales. There are still more than one thousand bales, which must be shipped to the end of the day. It is estimated that there are already spring cocoons, which have already been completed, a total of only six thousand bales, including summer cocoons, which is a decrease of six tenths compared to previous years. It has also been found that this year's Zhejiang and Anhui box tea is currently in the peak transportation season. It has been shipped since May, and has been reported to Shanghai through the Gate Station, and as of yesterday, there were 97,058 bales unloaded at the South Station, and more than 10,000 boxes at the North Station, all of which were inspected and released by customs officials. They were transported by truck to the Yuanji Foreign Warehouse on the Suzhou River for storage, and then gradually declared for export, mainly selling to foreign countries. It is reported that the estimated number of these goods is at least 200,000 boxes.

Report on the Survey and Acceptance of the Repair of Fu Gong Embankment in Huai'an

Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Association and Jiangsu Disaster Prevention Association Cooperate

In Huai'an County, Jiangbei, there is an embankment built by Prefect Tai in the Former Qing Dynasty. The people were grateful and named it Fu Gong Embankment. It is dedicated to resisting the waters of the Hongze, Baima, and Shiying Lakes, protecting 8,000 acres of fertile land and the lives of 100,000 people. It collapsed two years ago due to rising water and has not been repaired. This spring, the accumulated snow was very deep and summer floods are expected to be severe. Therefore, in March, the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association of this port raised 30,000 yuan and the Jiangsu Disaster Prevention Association allocated 10,000 yuan to repair it together. The project was entrusted to Wang Shuxiang and Tian Luyu to preside over, and it has been completed after three months. County Magistrate Zhang Zanxun of Huai'an County has accepted the report. The original text is recorded below: "On the night of June 18th, we received a telegram from your association stating that the Fu Embankment construction has been completed and that you requested us to conduct a nearby inspection and prepare the original and duplicate receipts, which were delivered to the two directors, Wang and Tian, to be sent to the association. We visited the Huayang Yizhenghui Jiangsu Disaster Prevention Association, etc. because the county magistrate went to inspect on the 24th. It was found that the main work of the Fu Gong Embankment, from the Zhenhu Bridge in the first section to the Shihandong in the 51st section, was 3,737 zhang and six cun long. The original plan for the new embankment was to have a top height of one zhang and three chi four cun and a width of one zhang. The new slope should be one wu inside and two wu outside. This survey found that the top width was at least one zhang and five cun, and most of them were one zhang and two chi, and some even reached one zhang and three chi. The height and slope were no less than the original plan. Moreover, the auxiliary works from the end of the Fu Embankment Shihandong, west to Sunzhuang, totaled ten sections, with a total length of 2,250 zhang. The length, width, height, and depth were also found to be consistent with the original plan. I have investigated that the Fu Gong Embankment externally defends against the waters of the Baima, Bao Ying, and Guangzhu Lakes, and internally protects thousands of acres of land in Huai and Huai counties. It is the largest embankment in Jiangbei. The new project is a total of 5,987 zhang long, with a total of 55,280 square meters of earth (the main project of the Fu Embankment accounts for two-thirds of the water area, and it takes three or four people to take one side of the soil in the water every day). A total of 121,000 man-days were recruited (construction started on April 2 and was completed on the 16th, with an average of 1,600 man-days per day). If laborers were hired, it would cost 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. It is now reported that the construction bureau only used more than 22,000 yuan including administrative fees. The new embankment is more than 30 li long, wide, high, and deep, and is uniform. According to the local elders, since the establishment of the Fu Embankment, there has never been such a high, wide, and solid one. Even if there is another 20 years of floods, it will be safe. The people will celebrate a new life forever, which is due to the kindness of your association. Director Wang Shuxiang was in charge of the construction and worked hard, and his perseverance and enthusiasm were admired by the people. Deputy Director Tian Luyu, who is over seventy years old, stayed at the construction site for three months, supervising and inspecting the project, experiencing hardships to complete the entire project, which is difficult for ordinary people to do. The supervising staff sent by the team leader also performed their duties diligently, and they did not disappoint the trust of your association, so they were able to accomplish this immortal feat together. Now, we are fortunate to see its completion and receive the telegram for inspection and acceptance. We are very grateful and respectfully represent the half-million disaster victims from five, six, and seven villages to thank you. In addition to preparing four original and duplicate receipts, which have been delivered to the two directors, Wang and Tian, we have reported the reasons for the telegram and the actual situation of the inspection and acceptance of the Fu Embankment. We have also enclosed a clear list of the new construction measurement尺交 delivered by the construction bureau for your review and approval."

Convenience for Passengers on Both Railways

丨Adding Chinese Food Sales to Passenger Cars丨

To provide convenience for passengers, the Ministry of Railways plans to add Chinese cuisine options to passenger cars on various railway lines. It has instructed both railway bureaus to order their traffic departments to quickly prepare. However, implementing this fully at once would require renovating kitchen cars, which would take time and money. To ensure practical and swift implementation, it is proposed to pilot this on the four daily special express trains with the highest passenger volume on both lines. Meanwhile, plans are still underway to implement this on all trains, and six articles of implementation measures have been drafted. In addition to submitting these to the ministry for approval, instructions have been issued to first add as much Chinese-style food and drink as possible before the pilot implementation. All preparations should be completed quickly for realization. To facilitate implementation, it is planned to start with the 4th and 1st special express trains departing in the morning on the Shanghai-Nanjing line, and the 2nd and 31st special express trains departing in the morning on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line. After achieving success, this will be gradually expanded to all trains. The existing kitchen spaces in the current dining cars are not suitable for selling Chinese food. The existing kitchen cars are at one end of the first-class cars, and their equipment is only suitable for preparing Western food, making it difficult to prepare Chinese food. It is planned to re-plan and renovate the kitchen spaces of four existing dining cars for this purpose. However, before the kitchen car renovations are completed, to meet the need, efforts will be made to attach two dining cars to each Jinghu special express train on both lines to temporarily provide Chinese and Western food. Also, Chinese cooking stoves are different from Western cooking stoves. It is planned to imitate the iron stove methods of Shanghai restaurants and hire workers to package them separately. Chinese cooking utensils are more complex than Western cooking utensils, requiring a total procurement cost of about 50 yuan per train. The ministry's specified utensils will be manufactured and applied in the same style. The methods for purchasing the above urgently needed utensils will be jointly reviewed and handled by the audit, materials, and traffic departments to ensure speed and practicality.

Zhabei District Fire Brigade Strives for Fire Safety

丨New Chinese Area Telephone Installed: 42255丨

The Zhabei District Section 3 Fire Brigade in this port has been established for more than twenty years and has made significant achievements in protecting the lives and property of citizens. Whenever the brigade hears of a fire, it immediately determines the address, dispatches vehicles, rushes to the scene, and makes every effort to rescue and extinguish the fire. To achieve this goal, it has long been praised by all sectors of Zhabei for its bravery and efforts. However, the brigade's area is adjacent to the concession, with many shops and dense populations, making it constantly worrisome. The brigade originally had a Chinese area telephone with the number 42255. It is now reported that the brigade director, to quickly communicate fire alarms in both the Chinese and foreign areas, has installed a concession telephone with the number 45588. If there are any fires or other incidents in the Chinese or foreign areas, the brigade should be notified using the above telephone numbers, and it will immediately determine the location, dispatch vehicles, and rush to the rescue. If there are any lawless individuals who falsely report fires, such behavior will disrupt fire safety. Their origins will be investigated and reported to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Chief for strict detention in accordance with the Regulations on Endangering Public Security to maintain fire safety and ensure local peace.
