Near-Term Gold Exchange Rate Discovered

A Short-Lived Reaction

After opening lower in the morning, a sharp squeeze led to a strong rebound. After the market began to decline, it eventually returned to a slight decrease of three yuan and three jiao. Although the gold market opened lower yesterday morning, it gradually rose after the opening, and the squeeze was extremely fierce. The quoted price was inverted by about ten yuan. The market first fell and then recovered. Early in the morning, both British and American silver prices rose, and the exchange rate rose frequently.

The forward silver price on the Gold and Silver Exchange rose from 1.5 fen to 1.85 fen. American cotton prices fell, while stocks rose. The raw silk market fell from over seventy yuan to sixty-five or sixty-six yuan. After opening, the banks forcefully supported it, and the situation stabilized. The HSBC exchange rate was announced, with the British pound at 25 and the US dollar at 875, already rising and recovering. Then, due to aggressive short covering, the gold price successively broke through the seventy and eighty yuan marks. The quoted price had already been exceeded, and the midday close rose again to over ninety yuan. However, the banks had no intention to sell. The afternoon session opened lower and fell further as the banks unloaded, but people were unsettled. However, those who took advantage of the low price to buy were strong, and with the two declines in Bombay totaling three annas, it was still able to recover in the end. It was still low at the close. It was found that the situation was extremely sharp throughout the day. The morning actually created a record of the lowest opening price and the highest closing price. This was also a reaction after continuous downstream losses. The industry was seeking to settle US dollars, and the banks were particularly sluggish. The swap price was approaching, and they had to cover their positions. In addition, under the aggressive purchase of speculator Wu, the sentiment was extremely firm. This swap happened to fall on a Saturday and was held earlier in the morning. Given today's situation, it seems difficult for the bulls to obtain a favorable premium, but it depends on the difference between the HSBC exchange rate and the quoted price of the US dollar. The raw gold price is subject to an additional two hundred and twenty yuan, which already has a source. The swap premium for July and August is seven yuan. Securities and Public Bonds Show Signs of Weakness

At the opening auction in the morning, various sectors remained firm. Although some Number 50 bonds were sold, it was not enough to stop the rise in prices, and new highs were seen for several stocks. Short-term financial public bonds, which usually saw little trading, suddenly experienced a demand of several hundred thousand in the early trading, pushing prices up by one yuan and several jiao, with the highest price reaching 66.4 yuan and 4 jiao. This was considered an anomaly and not indicative of the overall trend. In the second session, most stocks continued to show upward movement, but after 11:30 AM, long positions in Numbers 11, 32, and 50 bonds began to exit, gradually weakening prices. Salt taxes were no exception, falling by three to five jiao. Despite this, overall, gains still outweighed losses, but the trend showed signs of weakening. Sentiment remained high, making a sudden shift to pessimism unlikely, as the slight price fluctuations were mainly due to long positions exiting and hedging activities. Short sellers remained a minority, and the future outlook was expected to be a period of fluctuation. The total trading volume was 10,065,200 yuan, including 12,000 yuan in spot transactions and 3,310,000 yuan in futures for Tongfeng tax, 970,000 yuan for troop reduction, 1,100,000 yuan for 19 Customs bonds, 1,965,000 yuan for 20-year Customs bonds, 1,510,000 yuan for 96 bonds, and varying amounts from over ten thousand to over four hundred thousand for other issues.

Mills Compete to Replenish This Month's Flour

|| Outside traders compete to purchase forward contracts || Yesterday, the flour market showed signs of weakness in the morning after opening, as quotations for foreign wheat showed a small decline of three or four jiao for Zhima wheat and a few fen for Kan wheat. Given the rebound from the previous day and the flat sales, opening prices were also down by a fraction of a fen, with the lowest price for this month at two yuan, three jiao, two fen, two li and a half. But mills became active to cover their short-term needs, so the market became stable. By the afternoon opening, prices suddenly soared, because mills believed that inland wheat prices had not eased and rose as soon as there was movement. Although the recent sales of flour have not been very smooth, the blended price will inevitably result in a loss, so they let go and fully replenished. Only the market atmosphere in this month was exceptionally good. Forward contracts were also enthusiastically bought by outside traders, and gradually increased. However, Tianjin traders took the opportunity to sell back, in quantities of over 100,000 bags, which was also an incredible event. As a result, this month rebounded by one fen and two li and a half compared to the previous day, January rose by one fen and two li and a half, September rose by one fen and seven li and a half, October and November rose by one fen and a half, and December rose by two fen.

Inland Quotes Rise Sharply

Both Futures and Spot Wheat Stiffen

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning, prices had once eased, with Zhima wheat quotations down a small amount of three or four jiao and Kan wheat a few fen, so opening prices were down a fen or two for near-term contracts and stable for far-term contracts. Later, because the need to cover short positions was very urgent, opening prices rose again. By the afternoon opening, inland quotes had risen sharply, and holders of expensive goods were reluctant to sell cheaply. Medium-quality goods did not meet standards, and those who sought to arbitrage could only recover their costs, so the market felt particularly good and buying was very active. Looking at the subsequent situation, if the mill demand is good, prices are expected to continue to rise. As a result, this month rose by six fen compared to the previous day, August rose by four fen, September rose by five fen, October rose by four fen, November rose by six fen, and December rose by four fen. Spot wheat prices stiffened due to rising prices in the production areas and holders of goods were reluctant to sell. High-quality goods rose by an estimated three to five fen, while medium-quality goods remained flat. All Silk Mills in the City Reduce Working Hours Due to Summer Heat

Every summer, the city's silk mills reduce working hours by half. Starting yesterday, all 55 silk mills in the city only work half a day in the morning and stop work in the afternoon.

For the matter of announcement, Wei Huaishi and others have filed a petition requesting the issuance of a certificate of custodianship for the estate, stating in brief that the petitioner Wei Huaishi is the widow of the deceased Wei Qingtao. The petitioners Wei Nai, Xue, and were the sons of Qingtao. The petitioners Peilan and Zhulan were the daughters of Qingtao. The petitioner Youtang was the adopted son of Qingtao. Qingtao had a will dated June 8, 1920, stipulating the method of disposing of the estate and appointing Hua Guang, Zheng Shi, and Weng Fangquan and other interested parties as standing members of the estate trustees. Now, Qingtao unfortunately passed away on October 1, 1922. Among the properties left behind are several locations registered under British Deeds No. 2315, measuring 4 fen and 2 hao of land, No. 6207, measuring 4 mu, 1 fen, 1 li, and 1 hao of land, No. 968 of the American Deed, measuring 1 mu, 1 fen, 2 li, and 4 hao of land, and No. 1030, measuring 7 fen, 8 li, and 5 hao of land, which are all registered with the British firm Tonghe Foreign Firm. Therefore, this notice is made to inform the public. If anyone has objections to this request, they must come to the court to declare their objections within twenty days from the date of this announcement until the cessation of the announcement. If no one declares any objection within the time limit, this court will immediately issue a certificate of custodianship for the estate. This is hereby announced on June 30, 1922 of the Republic of China. 4491 Yi B

Commentary

The Longing for "First Prize"

— Bin Fu

If someone is deeply studying the Chinese national character, I believe that the recent "modern trend" prevailing in Chinese society cannot be ignored, otherwise, it will be difficult to have a deep understanding of the Chinese nation. What is the "modern trend"? This "modern trend" is neither the Three Principles of the People, nor nationalism, nor anarchism, but the "what if I won the first prize" reverie that often surges in people's minds recently.

Although I dare not say that every Chinese is fantasizing about "what if I won the first prize", I am afraid that there are not a few people who are fantasizing about "what if I won the first prize". Because in fact, millions or hundreds of thousands of lottery tickets have found their way, which is enough to see people's enthusiasm for buying lottery tickets. Since there is the motivation to buy tickets, who would not have the thought of "what if I won the first prize"?

The date of the aviation lottery draw is getting closer and closer. The aviation industry is fiddling with the abacus, planning how to use this "500,000" to operate another business! The worker in the factory is thinking about how to take the money to a large hotel to open a room and have fun. The bank clerk is smiling at the lottery ticket, thinking about how to buy a car and take revenge on the section chief and director. The contributor puts down the pen, thinking about how to use tens of thousands of yuan to run a magazine, so as to avoid the embarrassment of being ridiculed. The rickshaw puller also thinks that if the lottery ticket he bought together with his companions for a dime wins the first prize, he can get 5,000 yuan, and then he doesn't have to do the legwork of a rickshaw puller anymore. People of all classes are dreaming of their own interests, and people of all classes are longing for the "beautiful" gold. However, people of all classes spend their blood-stained money or savings, pursuing the "beautiful" gold hidden in the "first prize" like catching jade crabs in golden snails, but the "beautiful" gold hidden in the "first prize" will not and cannot fall in love with every individual who buys lottery tickets. This group of pitiful worms who rush to it and drool are just cherishing a "one-sided love" for the "golden" girl who is like a grain of sand in the Ganges. Here, the Chinese people's cleverness in gambling and speculation is nakedly exposed, but at the same time, it also shows the Chinese people's stupidity in not understanding the "probability".

The day of the lottery draw will arrive in the blink of an eye. When that time comes, the thermometer temperature may drop a little due to the public's disappointment.
